<time>1549253938434<//time><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
I live 5 minutes from its current location on White Oak and Lassen, and having ordered pizza, wings and salad from there over the last three years,  I confidently recommend Pizzasaurus Rex!

For the price, usually discounted with daily specials they offer, the pizza quality is far above the price. It's a pleasant surprise, and a great alternative to Papa John's, Pizza Hut and Little Ceaser's.

The older gentleman with glasses, presumable the owner, is a delight to deal with. He's courteous, polite and a friendly face.

RECOMMENDED PIZZA CHOICE:  medium pizza with extra sauce, pepperoni, pineapple and thick crust.

If you're in the area or searching for quality pizza, give Pizzasaurus a shot.< /review>

Great spot for dog grooming.
I just adopted a small dog from the shelter and he needed a hair cut.

I Called Doggie Ave, the person that answered the phone was very friendly and quoted a price that was very fair and in line with a couple of other places that I called.
I looked for a groomer in my area of Sherman oaks or North Hollywood but many places didn't answer or were closed on Monday.
I choose doggie Ave in Burbank

Luckily for me they had a cancellation and were able to fit me in that day.
what sold me was when I came in, I was greeted so nicely. Im a new owner to a long hair dog so this is a new experience for me.
It was a pleasure to have someone really listen to what I wanted done to my new dog.
They called me just as my dog Sammy was finishing so that he wouldn't have wait in a cage too long.

The hair cut shave that I asked for came out  awesome!!
THANKS!
Nice facility,  clean smelling, beautiful store with cute dog apparel and toys.
I will definitely be back.<//text>

<Date>1380583266950<//Date>< Text>
Today was the last straw for me with this place. I have been to this place on various occasions throughout the past two years for small items that I needed when in a bind and my supplier couldn't get it to me in time. And every time walked out empty handed and irritated. The sad part is I live 3 minutes away from this place and would rather drive to Rancho Cucamonga and shop at the candy supply store there then waste 1 penny on this place.

3 Reasons they received a 1 Star rating:

1) The store is small and very cluttered. The organization of the store will leave you wandering aroud trying to find everything.

2) All of the reviews about rudeness is true. The arrogance and inconvenience felt is very evident from everyone who works there.

3) This is the one that irritates me the most. The information given to customers in regards to Chocolate. I am not sure about their cake information they give out but as a professional chocolatier, I take great offense by the information they give their customers about chocolate. Merkins chocolate is in no way shape or form better than real chocolate. In a day when eating healthier is better and on the forefront of many peoples minds, Merkins chocolate which has 10+ ingredients (none of which are closely related to chocolate, in fact cocoa in most cases is not even an ingredient) is not better than the real chocolate which has at most 5 ingredients most of which is chocolate derivatives (i.e. cocoa powder, cocoa liquer, etc.) and the taste is WAY much better then the Merkins stuff. Also, with real chocolate and the Merkins "chocolate" you can add real ingredients into it for flavoring  (i.e. liquor, real fruits and such) unlike what the class tells you where "nothing can be added to chocolate except for oils because it will seize up" Wrong Wrong Wrong!!!

When a customer asks "How long will it take for the chocolate to set after dipping?" Don't answer, "Depending on room temperature, it should take no more than 5 minutes" Any type of chocolate, Merkins or the real deal cannot set properly at temps higher than 73 degrees, especially here in California. We don't have to worry about humidity as much but chocolate will take forever if at all to set at higher temperatures. Room Temperature is not a correct answer, in fact it is a very generalized answer that can and will ruin the chocolate confections you make if taken in the wrong context.

If you are here for cakes have fun, if you are here for chocolate turn around and run.</Text>

I wanted to share a history I I have with Curley or as we used to call it Curley's. My mother, Odette, used to cook here in the 1930's!  As a child, I performed with Disney and did appearance with Bob Hope and Danny Kaye. We ALWAYS went by Curley's after the appearances for a burger and Shirley Temple for me! A true institution, with the best customers around! BTW, Odette was fired one night for having a drink behind the bar at closing time, but she was hired back the next day!</Review>

< Date>
1562109828328<//Date>
<Text>Having lived just down the road from this Signal Hill institution for more than 15 years, it's odd that only after having moved a few miles away I would be drawn in to routinely dining here.  So, what's up you ask? For years  My parents and some good friends of theirs have made Wednesday evenings at Curley's apart of their routine. Although often invited, It was so routine that nothing seemed pressing about joining them. That was until my fine folks retired to Oregon and now seeing them was far less often and no longer on a whim the way I was used too. So, when they came to town and were wrapped up in catching up with old friends you can bet that Wednesday evening they were heading to Curley's. This was an invite I couldn't pass up, and now more than ever understand how good company, along with excellent food, served by one heck of a personable waiter named Jason and awesome live entertainment for a reasonable amount were so compelling. This is traditional diner food served in portions and prepared in a way you don't find often these days. The entertainment is usually a duet banjo and tuba with vocals from both mixed in. Usually American standards from the 1920's (roaring 20's) with sing a longs (lyrics provided to every table), the crowd of anywhere from 20 to 60 people are welcoming and a jovial bunch, and the atmosphere is so infectious it's impossible to imagine anybody not joining in for a thundering chorus of "she'll be coming round the mountain, when she comes". On evenings when the duet isn't available they are covered by the likes of a very talented Barbershop Quartet, or a sit in artist. But if this kind of "all in" audience participation live entertainment isn't exactly your thing, no need to hesitate; the front dining room and bar are left to the charms of what ever commentary patrons may have to what ever sports game is being aired on the TV monitors where there is no expectation of participation. The food and service are well worth giving Curley's a try. I regret waiting over 15 years to find out.</Text>< user_id>

< text>
We had a party of four adults and one child last evening. The food is always great, as my wife and I eat there often. We love Curleys; however, looking at my bill this morning, I noticed that they added an 18% gratuity to our bill of $91.16 or a total of $106.15, with tip.
Usually a tip is added for party‚Äôs of 8 or more and is stated on the menu. The waiter never told us there was an automatic tip added and I gave my usual 20% tip on top of $106.15.
I feel the waiter should have told us of the automatic tip. What restaurant automatically adds an 18% tip for only 5 people?
Everyone better check his ‚ÄúCurleys Bill‚Äù for the automatic tip. I know I will.......that is why the One Star Rating.</text>
